VI-1 Ex. (393)—1
THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION CHEPAUK, CHENNAI-600 005.
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
 NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LAND FOR 
INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997
(CLA-TID/2024/03/01/13/0001)
No.VI(1)/800(a-1)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 9.7500 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for TIDCO - 
New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO (LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO-New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.8100 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO-New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO (LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-TID/2024/03/05/18/0001)
No.VI(1)/800(a-3)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land 
for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 12.1350 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
TIDCO - New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit ,Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

(CLA-TID/2024/03/07/29/0001)
No.VI(1)/800(a-4)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to TIDCO - New Green Field Airport and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Managing 
Director, TIDCO. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of 
Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 9.6500 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for TIDCO - 
New Green Field Airport.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Kancheepuram and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Kancheepuram which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

28	
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
(LA-I(1)/9012864/2024)
No.VI(1)/800(a-6)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below to be 
acquired for Industrial Purposes to wit to Doubling of Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Eraniel and Parassala in 
Thickanamcode Village of Kalkulam Taluk in Kanniyakumari District, and it having already been decided that the amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Southern 
Railways. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for 
Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring 15323 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purposes wit, for the Doubling of 
Broad-Gauge Railway Line between  Eraniel and Parassala in Thickanamcode Village of Kalkulam Taluk in Kanniyakumari 
District.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the District Collector, Sub-Collector/ Revenue Divisional Officer, 
Kanniyakumari which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
The Schedule
Kanniyakumari District, Kalkulam Taluk, Thickanamcode Village.

Total
15323
Total Extent to be Acquired: 15323 Sq.mtrs.
(LA-III(2)/8914798/2024 )
No.VI(1)/800(a-7)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the land specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for Industrial Purpose to wit, for setting up SIPCOT Industrial Complex Phase-II and it having already been decided 
that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the land is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999). 
NOTICE
  Under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 0.26.00 Hectare to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purposes wit, for setting 
up SIPCOT Industrial Complex Phase-II.
 The plan of the land is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Office (LA), Allikulam Oil Refinery Industry 
Formation, SIPCOT Complex, Thoothukudi which may be inspected on any day during office hours.
